 '2017 main counselling ke dauraan mujhe jo fees bataai gai thi uske anusaar tution fees 8 lakh 55 hazaar or hostel fees 2 lakh rupye thi
 After this, when i came to join the college, the index college management asked me for two lakh rupees in the name of cash money and extra-curricular activity
 chunki main madhyamvargeey parivaar se hum isliye atirikt fees nahin chukaa sakati thi lekin neet pariksha ke baad bamushkil mila piji karne kaa ye avasar haath se naa nikal jaae isliye maine do lakh kaa phir lone liya
 After this, as soon as i arrived to join the college management again demanded two lakh rupees
 iske baad raat bhar ke prayaas ke baad maine apni seat khone ke dar se maine vyavastha bhi kii lekin college ne tution fees 8 lakh 55 hazaar se 9 lakh 90 hazaar kar di or sabhi chaatro se yah fees jamaa karne ko bolaa
 Apparently, it was difficult for everyone to bear the one lakh and 35 thousand fee increase, so all of us went against it to Jabalpur High Court
 iske baad college prabandhan ne mujhe vyaktigat taur par pratadit karnaa shuru kar diya
 Apart from this, on the phone, i was threatened to withdraw this case
 iske baad court ne index college ko nirdhaarit fees lene kaa aadesh diya lekin iske baad phir agle saal 9 lakh 90 hazaar rupye maangane lage
 
 
 i deposited only 8 lakh 55 thousand as per court order
 
 ' smriti or shivani donon baitool zile kii thim
 Both refer to the fees set in the suicide note
 donon maamalon main police jaanch karegi

 shivani ke pitaaji sab inspector hai
 Shivani was studying dental education
 uski bahan bhi embibies kii padhai pard rahi he
 No leader will say when the robbery will stop in the name of fees in the private medical college

 is baat kaa khulaasa ek research report se hua he jise KGI security analist 'ming shi ko' ne jari kiya he
 Interestingly, they are considered to be Apple's most accurate analysts in the world
 unhone apane research notemen kaha he ki appal ne iphone 7 Plus ke do varjan kii testing kii he jisamen se ek single lens camera he
 While the other is a dual lens setup
 haalanki company dul lens seoup ko 3di photo or depth of field vaale photo capchar karne ke liye istemaal nahin karegi
 He also said that the company will use dual lens setup to zoom in, which will provide a very strong optical zoom
 appal ne pichley saal camera technology company linx kharidi thi jiske jariye yphone main rier dul camera banaaya jayega
 It also appears from Ming Xi's report that the company has not yet decided whether the iphone 7 Plus will have a single rear camera or dual rear camera
 iske alaava appal ke vishleshak jon grabar ne 2014 ke aakhir main is baat kii taraf ishaara kiya tha ki appal apane future yphone main dul rier camera seoup laa saktaa he
 However, nothing has been said about the dual camera setup from the company
 appal sitambar yaa oktober main nayaa yphone launch karegi

 congress ne dilli, madhya pradesh or rajasthan vidhansabha chunaavon main paraajay ko sweekaar kiya or kaha ki vah chunaav nateezon se niraash he

 ham sweekaar karte hai ki ham vahaan haar gayi hai

 He said that any celebration before the 2014 Lok Sabha elections would be inopportune
 bijepi itihaas se sabak lene ko taiyaar nahin he

 mizoram bhi achche parinaam laaegi

" iske kaarnon kii samiksha kii jaaegi
 ' raipur ke kai ilaakon main winter diaria kaa atake hua he
 Hundreds of children under one year have become ill from its virus
 bataaya ja rahaa he ki thand main kai bachche rota virus kii chapet main aae hai
 Forty to fifty such children are being treated daily in government hospitals, who have been found to have winter diarrhea positive
 medical jaanch main aise bacchon ke khun main rota virus paaya gaya he
 Doctors have advised to save children below one year of age from cold
 unke mutabik sardi badhane ke chalate rota virus active he
 Not only this, due to pollution in the environment, this virus is getting a chance to flourish
 darasal raipur ke chaaron ore audyogig ikaiyaan hai
 Most industrial units produce iron
 inamen se sabase khatarnaak sapanj aayran udhog he
 Here coal and furnace oil are used extensively for making iron
 isse nikalne vaala dhuna din bhar vaataavaran main maujuud rahata he
 In the cold weather, this smoke comes towards the ground surface instead of going towards the sky
 iske alaava vaataavaran main maujuud dhul ke kanon se bhi logon ko swasth sambandhi bimaariyaan ho rahi hai
 At the same time, most of the young children are suffering from pollution this season
 raipur ke tamaam sarkari or gaiyr sarkari asapatalon main rojaanaa winter diaria se grashit 50 nae cese darj ho rahe he
 Whereas, the administration does not have any data of those treated in non-government hospitals and private dispensaries
 doctoron ke mutabik nijee aspataalon main ilaaj karaane vaale bacchon kii sankhya sarkari aspataalon se kahin zyada he
 Doctors have warned people in this season to avoid taking children below one year out of the house
 kendriya mantri nitin gadakari ne loksabhaa chunaav se thik pehle ab ek aisa bayaan diya he jisase unheen kii sarkaar kii mushkilen bad sakati hai
